=== SEARCH SNIPPETS ===

[Yepishata - Wikipedia]
Yepishata (Russian: Епишата) is a rural locality (a village) in Klyapovskoye Rural Settlement, Beryozovsky District, Perm Krai, Russia. The population was 33 as of 2010. Yepishata is located on the Barda River, 26 km east of Beryozovka (the district's administrative centre) by road.
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yepishata

[PDF RUSSIA / РОССИЯ, ROSSIYA 2010 CENSUS - East View]
East View presents the Russia 2010 Census as part of the East View Global Census Archive® (GCA). The Russia 2010 Census addresses a wide range of topics at the highest level of detail possible.
URL: https://www.eastview.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Russia_2010Census_Factsheet.pdf

[ACCORDING | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary]
Phrasal verb accord with something (Definition of according from the Cambridge Advanced Learner's Dictionary & Thesaurus © Cambridge University Press)
URL: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/according

[2010 Russian census - Wikipedia]
The census recorded the population as 142.9 million, a decrease of 2.3 million (1.6%) since the 2002 census. The population is 73.7% urban (105.3 million) and 26.3% rural (37.5 million).
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2010_Russian_census

[Russia 2010 Census Data Collection - East View Census GIS Data ...]
East View Geospatial has reprocessed data from All-Russia 2010 Population Census (Всероссийская перепись населения - 2010) published by Rosstat, the Federal State Statistics Service (Федеральная служба государственной статистики (Росстат)).
URL: https://guides.library.upenn.edu/EastViewCensusGIS/Russia2010CensusData

--- [Yepishata - Wikipedia] ---
Yepishata (Russian: Епишата) is a rural locality (a village) in Klyapovskoye Rural Settlement, Beryozovsky District, Perm Krai, Russia. The population was 33 as of 2010.

--- [2010 Russian census - Wikipedia] ---
The 2010 Russian census (Russian: Всеросси́йская пе́репись населе́ния 2010 го́да) was the second census of the Russian Federation population after the dissolution of the Soviet Union. Preparations for the census began in 2007 and it took place between October 14 and October 25.


--- [Russia 2010 Census Data Collection - East View Census GIS Data ...] ---
East View Geospatial Census Data Collection products are licensed by the Penn Libraries for the use of current Penn students, faculty, and staff. If you are not affiliated with the University of Pennsylvania, then you should contact your library for access through their collections or contact East View. East View Geospatial has reprocessed data from All-Russia 2010 Population Census (Всероссийская перепись населения – 2010) published by Rosstat, the Federal State Statistics Service (Федеральная служба государственной статистики (Росстат)). This data product provides 139 census data variables demographic, economic, housing, migration (ethnicity), social, and transportation characteristics. The data product does not include every variable collected by the Russian census. The smallest geographic unit of analysis for these variables is ADM3, Third-Order Administrative Division, with variables for ADM2, Second-Order Administrative Division. A parallel series of shapefiles provides ADM3 and ADM2 coverages. Geographic variables for Cyrillic and transliterated placenames and codes are provided for 2,228 ADM2 - District (raion or city district) - and 21,659 ADM3 - Rural Councils (selsoviet), settlements, and towns - geographic areas. East Vew Geospatial has published the dataset in two formats: two ArcGIS geodatabase; six pairs of ArcGIS shapefiles, corresponding to thematic content for ADM2 and ADM3 geographic coverage. The dataset is projected as WGS1984. For Second-Order and Third-Order Administrative Divisions. Attribute variables include : Total population. Urban population. Rural population. Population, natural change (percent). Total female population. Total male population (persons). Female (age groups) : age 0-2; 3-5; 6; 7; 8-13; 14-15; 16-17; 18-19; 20-24; 25-29; 30-34; 35-39; 40-44; 45-49; 50-54; 55-59; 60-64; 65-69; 70 and older. Male (age groups : age 0-2; 3-5; 6; 7; 8-13; 14-15; 16-17; 18-19; 20-24; 25-29; 30-34; 35-39; 40-44; 45-49; 50-54; 55-59; 60-64; 65-69; 70 and older. For Second-Order and Third-Order Administrative Divisions. Attribute variables include : Average salary (rubles). Average government salary (rubles). Number of families that have applied for subsidies. Personal income tax (rubles). Occupation : Agriculture; Forestry; Fishing; Aquaculture ; Mining ; Manufacture ; Utilities ; Construction ; Wholesale Trade; Retail ; Hospitality ; Transportation; Communications ; Finance ; Real Estate ; Government ; Education ; Healthcare; Other Services. Nurses employed in state facilities.; Nurses employed in private facilities. Doctors employed in state facilities; Doctors employed in private facilities. For Second-Order and Third-Order Administrative Divisions. Attribute variables include : Private household size: Average; Total; 1 Member; 2 Members; 3 Members; 4 Members; 5 Members. Total housing (square meters). Persons residing in deteriorating housing. Total new housing (square meters). New individual housing (square meters). Number Of settlements without access to natural gas. For Second-Order and Third-Order Administrative Divisions. Attribute variables include : Population migration change.Ethnicity : Russian; Tatars; Chuvash; Ukrainians; Bashkirs; Chechens; Udmurt; Armenians; Avars; Mordvins; Mari; Kazakh; Komi; Ossetians; Buryats; Dargins; Kumyks; Kabardians; Tuvans; Adyghe; Lezgins; Germans; Azerbaijanis; Belarusians; Kalmyk; Laks; Romani; Balkars; Turkish; Koreans; Nogais; Khakas; Uzbek; Karelians; Nenets; Ingush; Greek; Shors; Khanty; Rutul; Aghul; Tajik; Cossacks; Kurds; Kryashens; Karachays; Kyrgyz; Evenks; Nanai; Koryaks; Tanzanian; Georgians; Other; Not specified.
